id=\"section_460\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/30119962/\">460.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Whenever a document is withdrawn from the record, whether before or after judgement, a note shall be made in the column of remarks, stating also whether a copy has or has not been substituted.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_461\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/183086265/\">461.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Individual documents are not to be shown in the table of contents. The lists which are attached to them will alone be shown in this table, and will bear serial and sheet numbers.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_462\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/125665947/\">462.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When File A contains parties' documents the reader shall write \"Returnable Documents\" in red ink on the title page before sending the records to the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_463\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/158022910/\">463.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Documents tendered in evidence but not put on the record do not form part of the record. They shall whenever possible be returned forthwith to the person by whom they were tendered or to his pleader. Rejected documents which cannot be retuned earlier shall be returned by post or otherwise as the Court may order, after the conclusion of the trial but before the record is deposited in the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_464\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/92519751/\">464.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Strong covers shall be used for protecting the documents put on the record on behalf of each party. The best form of cover is a sheet of cartridge paper 19\" by 13 \u00bd\" bent double and guarding the documents on both sides.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_465\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/33576137/\">465.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When any map or plan is filed in a record it should be placed in a separate envelope so as to be easily removable for inspection. The envelope, and not the map or plan, should be attached to the record.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_466\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/74612761/\">466.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The Court shall make special provision for the safe custody during trial of any documents alleged to be urged and may make special provisions of the safe custody during trial of any document which by reason of antiquarian or other value it considers unsuitable for retention on the record. Documents known or suspected to be forged shall be kept in a sealed envelope bearing an endorsement describing its contents. The envelope shall be kept in the custody of the nazir (or naib-nazir) and on no account kept with the record. The Court shall make an entry in the order sheet whenever it sends the envelope to the nazir, and shall be responsible for its safe transit to and from his custody.</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_466.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/74685148/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Articles in Evidence</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_467\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/79907772/\">467.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When any article other than a document that can be filed with the record is produced it shall be marked by having attached to it a slip bearing a capital letter.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_468\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/132074576/\">468.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A list of the articles produced in evidence shall be prepared by the reader in Form No. 194 on Schedule V and shall be signed by the presiding officer. Articles shall be entered in the list in the order in which they are marked.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_469\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/13350076/\">469.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In a sessions case the Sessions Judge may either transfer the committing Magistrate's list to his own file and use it as his own list with amendments or additions or have a fresh list made out. In the latter case he shall, as far as possible, use the same letter for each article as the committing Magistrate.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_470\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/74227451/\">470.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Whenever an article entered in the list is disposed of, a note of the manner of disposal shall be made in the list.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">E.-General Rules</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_471\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/27815827/\">471.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Papers shall, as for as possible, be attached to the file to which they belong as the trial proceeds. The filing of papers in their proper files must in all cases be completed before the record is deposited in the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_472\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/71021853/\">472.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where an accused absconds and no separate miscellaneous proceeding under Section 512 of the Code is registered, the reader shall note \"Absconding accused\" on the title page in red ink.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_473\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/64406531/\">473.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The sheets in all files shall be numbered consecutively.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - In this connection, Please see Rule 461.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_474\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/39535119/\">474.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The table of contents to be used for the records of Criminal Courts is printed on the reverse side of the title page. Column 1 of the table shall contain the serial number of the various papers in the file, and column 2 shall contain against each such serial number the number of the sheets comprising it. The entries in columns 1 to 4 shall be made by the reader as the case proceeds, and the entry in column 5 by the record-keeper after the record has been deposited in the record room. In the table of contents for B files only the total number of sheets in the file need be shown.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_475\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/27208055/\">475.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If any paper is transferred from one file to another the transfer shall be noted in the remarks column of the table of contents of the old and the new files. A new sheet number and if necessary a new serial number shall be given in the table of contents of the new file.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-chapter\"><h2>Chapter 19<br/>The Transmission of Records and Other Papers to the Record Room for Custody</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">(The rules in this chapter have been made under Section 124 of the Government of India Act)</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_476\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/128884492/\">476.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">With the exception of proceedings before the Court of Session, the records of which will be kept in the criminal section of the District and Sessions Judge's record room, records of all criminal proceedings shall be kept in the record room of the District Magistrate.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Proceedings referred to the Court of Session under the Central Provinces Borstal Act (C.P. IX of 1928) or under Section 123 (2) of the Code or any similar provision of law shall for the purpose of this rule be regarded as proceedings in the referring Court.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">I.-The District Magistrate's Record Room</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A.-Records</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_477\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/102257828/\">477.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Proceedings are divided into three classes, original cases, miscellaneous judicial proceedings, and miscellaneous non-judicial proceedings. A list of miscellaneous judicial proceedings is given in Chapter 24, Rule 575, of Part IV. Proceedings of prosecution for offences against accused persons which are not classified in that list are original cases. Miscellaneous non-judicial cases are dealt with in Rule 402 (1) below.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_478\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/192023794/\">478.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_478.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/78851643/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The records of all cases registered in the register of original cases shall be sent by the reader of the Court through the statistical writer to the record-keeper as soon as possible after disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_478.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/149967791/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records of cases ending in a conviction under Section 34 (b) of the Police Act or under Section 118 (1) (a) (i) of the Governments Act (II of 1924) or under Section 510 of the Indian Penal Code shall be sent by the statistical writer to the District Excise Officer before passing them on to the record-keeper.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_479\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/155598151/\">479.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The records of enquiries preliminary to commitment and proceedings specified in the note to Rule 476 shall be sent by the reader of the Sessions Court through the District Magistrate to the record-keeper after the conclusion of the sessions trial.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_480\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/37352161/\">480.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The records of all proceeding registered as miscellaneous judicial proceedings and the records of appeals and revision shall be sent to the record-keeper as soon as possible after disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_481\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/160219245/\">481.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The monthly bundles of cases dismissed under Section 203 of the Code shall be sent with a list (in Form No. 21 on Schedule V) through the statistical writer to the record-keeper at the close of each month.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_482\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/72814743/\">482.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_482.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/106339702/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">All proceedings relating to the exercise of the functions of magistrates which are not original cases or miscellaneous judicial proceedings or proceedings in appeal or revision or proceedings relating to such proceedings are classified as miscellaneous non-judicial proceedings. The papers of such proceedings shall be made into two monthly bundles as directed below and sent by the reader with lists (in Form No. 22 on Schedule V) to the record keeper at the close of each month.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_482.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/117398831/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In one bundle shall be placed all police papers of a preliminary or informatory nature on which the Magistrate has passed orders (e.g., under Sections 62, 157, 173 and 174 of the Code and orders on applications under Section 344) 'also all applications for licenses under the Arms Act, Petroleum Act and Poisons Act and the list accompanying this bundle shall be marked A'.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">(No. 8 dated 5-12-51)</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_482.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/13768438/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In the other bundle shall be placed the records of other miscellaneous non-judicial proceedings [e.g., under Section 13 of the Indian Lunacy Act, or Section 18 of the Vaccination Act, or Section 77 (1) of the Central Provinces Municipalities Act, or Section 514 of the Code or proceedings under Sections 107 and 145 of the Code, dismissed in a preliminary enquiry or on a police report, or proceedings for the recovery of fines or for disposal of property]. The list of this bundle shall be marked B.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - District Magistrate should refer, for the orders of the High Court cases where there is doubt as to the inclusion of papers as miscellaneous non-judicial cases.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_483\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/24965613/\">483.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Documents known or suspected to be forged, and documents which are to be kept in special custody shall be sent by the reader to the record-keeper in a separate sealed envelope, for which the record-keeper shall give a receipt. The documents shall be kept in a special box under lock and key and a reference made in the record of the case to which they relate showing where they are kept.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_484\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/10124065/\">484.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">All papers which are to be included in the record of an original case or a miscellaneous judicial proceeding or a miscellaneous non-judicial proceeding which has already been deposited in the record room shall be sent to the record-keeper as occasion arises with a list (in Form No. 22 on Schedule V) giving particulars of the case to which they relate.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_485\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/124116923/\">485.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The District Magistrate shall give directions to ensure the safety of records in transit from one officer to another, and in particular he shall give directions for the issue of receipt for records so that responsibility for the loss of a record can be determined.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_486\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/31464310/\">486.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The principle underlying the arrangement of records in the record room is that, as far as possible, records shall be stored in the order of disposal without distinction of courts or classes of cases. The position of each record in the record room is traced by the number allotted to it in the record room register of criminal cases maintained by the record-keeper (in Form No. 83 on Schedule V) and for this purpose it is necessary to arrange, as far as possible, that registration of records in the register shall be made in the order of disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_487\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/97943209/\">487.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records as received from day to day shall be arranged in separate files according to the day of disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_488\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/133011641/\">488.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">On the 3rd of the month or other convenient date appointed by the District Magistrate each Court shall certify to the statistical writer whether all records disposed of in the previous month have been dispatched for deposit in the record room. The serial number and date of the disposal of any record which has not been so sent shall be intimated to the statistical writer.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_489\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/88052023/\">489.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">On the 7th of the month or other convenient date appointed by the District Magistrate the statistical writer shall send the record-keeper a statement based on the certificate referred to in Rule 488 indicating which records disposed of in the previous month have been forwarded to the record room and which have been kept back. On receipt of this certificate the record-keeper shall commence the registration of the records in the register of criminal cases.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_490\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/45627261/\">490.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records shall be entered as far as possible in the order of their disposal. Each record or monthly bundle entered in the register shall be given a number, which number shall be prominently inscribed by the record-keeper on the record. Appellate and revisional records and records of proceedings under Sections 250, 386 and 388 of the Code shall not be separately registered or given a separate number. Such record shall be filed with the record of the original case, and a not of the date and details of the final order in such proceedings shall be made in the appropriate column of the register against the entry for the original case.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_491\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/115994919/\">491.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records received in the record room too late for registration in the order of their disposal shall be entered at the end of the entries made in that month. Space should be reserved for belated entries in accordance with the information received under the provisions of Rule 488.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_492\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/86166705/\">492.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The entry in the register shall be made in accordance with the facts of the case. Thus, where proceedings under Section 145 of the Code are instituted by the police, the State shall be shown as the complainant and the contesting parties as the opposite party. Where the proceedings are instituted on the complaint of one of the contesting parties he shall be shown as the complainant and the other contestant as the opposite party.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_493\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/182958908/\">493.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If a record is sent out of the record room before it has been registered in the register of criminal cases a memorandum (in Form No. 149 on Schedule II) shall be kept in its place. Entries in the record room register should be made from the material in the memorandum and the serial number in the register allotted to the memorandum shall be reproduced on the record when it is returned.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_494\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/164294918/\">494.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">After registration groups of records, in chronological order of their registration, shall be done up in bundles with cloth wrappers. Each bundle shall be allotted a number and the wrapper shall bear a label showing the serial number of the bundle, the number allotted in the register to the records contained in the bundle and the month and year in which the cases were disposed of, thus:-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Bundle No. 25</span><span class=\"akn-p\">February and March 1939</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\"><h3>76. </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">-125</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_495\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/194827377/\">495.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">To secure uniformity in the making up of bundles of records and to economise space on the racks in record rooms the following instructions shall be followed:-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_495.i\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/159700622/\">(i)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The vertical space between one shelf and the next above is generally 18 inches of which 15 \u00bd inches are available for storing records, 2 \u00bd inches being taken up by the edge plate. Fourteen inches of this space should be filled, 1 \u00bd inches being left for the removal and replacing of bundles.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_495.ii\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/186148003/\">(ii)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Bundles shall be not less than six nor more than seven inches deep and shall be arranged in pairs one above the other, the depth of each pair not exceeding 14 inches. The above figures may be modified at the direction of the District Magistrate to suit racks in which the space between shelves is greater or less than 15 \u00bd inches.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_495.iii\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/139169328/\">(iii)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The cloth used for a bundle should be large enough to cover the records within it completely convenient dimensions for a 7\" bundle are 3 \u00bd' X 3 \u00bd'. To one corner of the cloth should be attached a piece of stout cotton twine of suitable length which, if passed tightly round the bundle breadthwise, will both keep it compact and exclude dust. Such twine can be had in most headquarter stations and its purchase in the local market is permissible under Stationery Rule 4. The practice of closing a bundle by tying the four corners is prohibited.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_496\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/180244648/\">496.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When from time to time records or portions of records are eliminated from the bundles in pursuance of the rules for the destruction of records contained in the next Chapter, records shall be re-grouped and made into fresh bundles in order to maintain the depth laid down in the preceding rule. Each fresh bundle shall be given a fresh label.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_497\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/52045111/\">497.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When a record is removed from the record room for any purpose, the record-keeper shall keep a memorandum (in Form No. 149 on Schedule II) in its place and shall enter in a register called, the record room register of dispatch of records (in Form No. 78 on Schedule II) a note of the number of the case, the names of the parties, the name of the Court or officer requiring its removal, and the date of the removal. On the return of the record he shall note in the same register the date of the return and remove the memorandum, restoring the record to its proper place.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - The signature of the receiving Court or officer, or, if that is not possible, of the clerk responsible for dispatching the record, shall be taken in the appropriate column of the register at the time of removal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_498\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/21363189/\">498.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In the first week of each month the record-keeper shall prepare and submit to the District Magistrate a list of records which, on the last day of the preceding month, had already been out of the record room, whether for the purpose of appeal or otherwise, for more than two months. If the list is blank a report to that effect shall be submitted for the District Magistrate's information. The list shall be destroyed after the expiry of three years from the date of the last entry, provided all the records entered therein have been received back in the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_499\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/190274206/\">499.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Whenever any record or part of a record is found missing a report shall be made at once by the record-keeper to the District Magistrate who shall cause an enquiry to be held without delay. Losses of an entire file and cases in which theft is suspected shall be reported through the Sessions Judge to the Registrar of the High Court as soon as the enquiry has been completed. The report shall contain a full statement of the measures taken to prevent losses of a like kind from recurring and also state whether the papers have been recovered or not and how the person, if any, held responsible has been dealt with.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A missing record is one which is not where it should have been had the proper procedure been followed and is not known to be in some proper custody elsewhere.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Clerks are strictly forbidden to take records home.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_500\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/100228672/\">500.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The record-keeper shall maintain a plan and an index showing the number and position of the racks, and the arrangement and number of the bundles in the record room and revise the index every year in the first week of July.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_501\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/166125421/\">501.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The duties of the record-keeper with regard to the cancellation of Court-fee stamps are laid down in Rule 556 of Chapter 22, Part III.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B.-Registers</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_502\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/19917580/\">502.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">All registers deposited in the record room shall be entered by the record-keeper in a register (in Form No. 79 on Schedule II) entitled register of registers deposited in the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_503\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/112401392/\">503.</a> The registers shall consist of three parts, viz.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">I. List of registered to be preserved for fifty years.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">II. List of registers to be preserved for period other than fifty years.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">III. List of registers deposited under Rule 510 (iii) (I).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_504\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/106365648/\">504.</a> </h3></section></section></section><section class=\"akn-part\"><h2>Part II \u2013 shall be divided into sections as follows:-</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Section A-Registers to be preserved for 14 years.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Section B-Registers to be preserved for 6 years.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Section C-Registers to be preserved for 3 years.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Section D-Registers to be preserved for 1 year.</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_505\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/142528840/\">505.</a> </h3></section></section><section class=\"akn-part\"><h2>Part I \u2013 and each Section of Part II shall be divided into groups by kinds of register only, the number of groups in each part or section being identical with that of the kinds of register included therein. A separate series of numbers shall be given to the registers in each group. Enough space shall be allotted to each group to last for a number of years. Part II may be split up into several volumes if convenient, provided that the sections in any given volume shall be complete in themselves.</h2>\n<section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_506\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/141864906/\">506.</a> </h3></section></section><section class=\"akn-part\"><h2>Part I \u2013 and each volume of Part II shall be paged throughout with an index at the beginning. The entries in the index to Part I shall be made in the order of the groups into which the part is divided, and those in the index to each volume of Part II shall be made in the order of sections as well as groups in the volume.</h2>\n<section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_507\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/35447622/\">507.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When registers are received in the record room the entries relating to them shall be made below the existing entries in the respective groups in Part I or Part II to which they belong.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_508\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/84691044/\">508.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When a new volume is opened care should be taken to ensure that the space allotted to each group in Part I or Part II is such that the pages belonging to all groups will be completely filled in approximately the same length of time.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_509\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/57761191/\">509.</a> [ <span class=\"akn-remark\" data-status=\"editorial\">[Omitted by High Court Notification No. 10539, dated 22-12-53.]</span>\n</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">* * *].</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_510\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/6975220/\">510.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-blockList\"><span class=\"akn-listIntroduction\">List of registers, etc., to be deposited in the criminal record room of District Magistrates. class=\"akn-p\">Intimations of fines realized (V-98).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(5)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Indents, offence ledger, etc.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">II.-The District and Session Judge's Record Room</span><span class=\"akn-p\">(Criminal Section)</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A. Records</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_511\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/49032782/\">511.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records of proceedings before the Court of Sessions whether decided by the Sessions Judge or an Additional Sessions Judge shall be forwarded by the reader of the Sessions Judge to the record-keeper as soon as possible after disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_512\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/41335878/\">512.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">All papers which are to be included in the record of proceedings already deposited in the record room shall be sent by the reader of the Judge concerned to the record-keeper as occasion arises.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_513\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/15006143/\">513.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Papers of miscellaneous proceedings of the nature of miscellaneous non-judicial proceedings shall be made into monthly bundles and sent with a list (in Form No. 22 on Schedule V) by the reader of the Judge concerned to the record-keeper at the close of each month.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_514\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/139057003/\">514.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">On the 3rd of each month or other convenient date appointed by the Sessions Judge the reader of the Sessions Judge shall certify to the record-keeper whether all cases disposed of in the previous month have been dispatched for deposit in the record room.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_515\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/134879779/\">515.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The record-keeper shall deal with the records on the principles laid down in the rules in Part I of this Chapter.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B. Registers</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_516\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/194516976/\">516.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The record-keeper shall deal with registers deposited in the record room on the principles laid down in the rules in Part I of this Chapter.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_517\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/164287817/\">517.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-blockList\"><span class=\"akn-listIntroduction\">List of registers, etc., to be deposited in the record room (criminal section) of District and Sessions Judges. The Schedule and form numbers are given in brackets :-</span><span class=\"akn-item\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(i)</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Court registers-</span></span></span></span><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/197216712/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Sessions trials register (V-79)</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/186476002/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Register of original miscellaneous proceedings (V-72).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/18795743/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Register of appeals (V-77)</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/148423347/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Register of revisions (V-78).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/179075386/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Fine register A (V-73).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/29963476/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Fine register B (V-74).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_517.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/79751286/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Register of process-fees and diet-money (V-75).</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_517.7.ii\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/195894424/\">(ii)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Record room registers-</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(1)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Registers of records deposited in the record room (11-79).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(2)</span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Record room register of criminal cases (V-83).</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(iii)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">General-</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(1)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Intimations of fines realized (V-98).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(2)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">List of jurors and assessors.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(3)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Cause lists, etc.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-chapter\"><h2>Chapter 20<br/>Destruction of Records</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">[The rules in this Chapter have been made under Section 3 of the Destruction of Records Act (V of 1917)]</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_518\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/15934836/\">518.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Except as provided in the rules next following the papers in A files shall be destroyed on the expiry of the period given below and the papers in file B at the end of six months. The period shall be calculated from the date of the final order in the case, whether the order be that of the Original Court or of a Court acting in appeal or revision or upon reference. In enquiries preliminary to commitment ending in commitment the final order in the trial as defined above shall be regarded as the final order in the enquiry.</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/24951560/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Sessions trials in which the final order is one of conviction-14 years.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/29213652/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Cases tried by a Magistrate in which the final order imposes or maintains a substantive sentence of imprisonment for more than 2 years-7 years.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/174769552/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Sessions cases in which the final order is one of acquittal, cases under Chapter VIII of the Code in which the final order is an order to give security, and all cases under Chapter XII of the Code-3 years.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/99623214/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Cases tried by a magistrate in which the final order is of discharge or acquittal or in which a complaint is dismissed under Section 204 (3) of the Code-1 year.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.e\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/83985163/\">(e)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Record of appeals or revisions deposited in the record room (criminal section) of the District and Sessions Judge-2 years.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_518.f\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/185090875/\">(f)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Enquiries preliminary to commitment and all other cases or proceedings not otherwise provided for in this list for which a separate record prepared-2 years.</span></span></section><span class=\"akn-wrapUp\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Records of appeals and revisions other than those referred to in clause (e) shall be destroyed along with the record of the original case.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_519\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/52305310/\">519.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The A files shall not be destroyed before the expiry of the sentence passed in the case or the death of the person sentenced to imprisonment, whichever is earlier.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_520\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/147605811/\">520.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The A file of a case in which an order is made for the detention of a person under the Indian Lunacy Act or the Indian Labels Act or for the making over of a lunatic to the custody of a friend or relation under the Indian Lunacy Act shall not be destroyed before the termination of that detention or custody by the death, release or recovery of the lunatic or leper.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_521\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/140670195/\">521.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The A file of a case in which an injunction has been issued under the Child Marriage Restraints Act shall not be destroyed till the child in respect of whom the injunction has been used has become a major. If there is no finding on the age of the child the record shall be destroyed after 14 years in the case of an injunction relating to a female and after 18 years in the case of an injunction relating to a male child.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_522\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/143559172/\">522.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_522.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/141859925/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In a case ending in conviction for an offence punishable under Chapter XII or XVII of the Indian Penal Code with imprisonment for a term of three years or more, the title page, charge-sheet, judgement, finding and sentence of the Trial Court and the judgement or order of the Appellate or Revisional Court shall be preserved till the convict is known to be dead.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_522.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/160391357/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The A file of a case in which any of the accused has not been apprehended shall be preserved till that person is known to be dead or till there is no longer any intention of proceeding against him.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_522.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/22727079/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The A file of a case in which an order for maintenance has been made under Section 488 of the Code shall be preserved till the person maintained is known to be dead or till it is known that the liability has ceased and no arrears are recoverable.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_523\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/126945148/\">523.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The records of cases referred to in Rules 520 and 522 shall, at the end of 20 years from the date of the final order, be examined by the District Magistrate who may order their destruction or fix a further period after which they are to be re-examined.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_524\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/75828426/\">524.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Monthly bundles of complaints dismissed and of miscellaneous non-judicial cases (list A) shall be destroyed at the end of one year from the date of the last order in the bundle. Miscellaneous non-judicial cases (list B) shall be destroyed at the end of three years from the date of the last order in the bundle.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_525\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/109604784/\">525.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Sessions Judges and District Magistrate may order the preservation of any particular record beyond the prescribed period.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - It is open to a Magistrate to refer to the District Magistrate any case in which he considers preservation beyond the prescribed time desirable; as where a Magistrate finds it necessary to discharge an accused in a case of forgery but considers the record or the document alleged to be forged requires extended preservation.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_526\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/71587732/\">526.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">On the judgement or order in any case becoming final, notice (in Form No. 99 on Schedule V) shall be given to any person who produced a document filed with the record, or to his counsel, requiring him to claim the document forthwith and warning him that in default the document will be destroyed with the record. A copy of the notice shall be exhibited in the court-room of the Court which dealt with the case.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Care must be taken that no document which has been impounded shall be delivered out of the custody of the Court.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_527\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/107870848/\">527.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The ordinary monthly inspection of the record room registers and bundles for the purpose of eliminating A and B files shall be supplemented by a monthly reference to the registers for 12 months further back, and such records as were held over during the first examination and are then due for destruction shall be eliminated.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_528\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/109639800/\">528.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Registers, returns and other papers shall be destroyed at the expiry of the period shown against them in column (2) of the subjoined table, such period being calculated from the date shown in that column :</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Provided that the record room register of criminal cases shall be destroyed only after all the records entered in it have been eliminated and that the register of original cases and of appeals containing entries of cases disposed of before the record room register of criminal cases in the revised form was introduced shall be preserved for 50 years.</span><div class=\"akn--table-container\"><table class=\"akn-table\" class=\"akn-p\">1 years from the end of the year to which they relate.</span></td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table></div></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_529\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/186120112/\">529.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A note of every paper, register or record taken out for destruction shall, at the time of removal, be made in the appropriate record room register and shall be initialled by the record keeper. If in any case destruction is not effected the note shall be cancelled under the record-keeper's initials. At the end of each calendar month the officer in charge of the record room shall see what papers have been taken out and pass order for their disposal.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_530\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/17195601/\">530.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Destruction, which shall ordinarily be by burning, shall be effected monthly under the supervision of the officer in charge of the record room. At stations where there is a district or central jail., the superintendent of which has certified that he will arrange for the prompt removal of waste paper, the District Magistrate may direct that all destruction shall be effected by tearing into small pieces. Before giving such a direction the District Magistrate shall satisfy himself that a proper receptacle for temporary storage of waste paper is available and shall take all other precautions necessary to minimise the risk of damage by fire to records which are to be retained.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_531\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/60173190/\">531.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The instructions in Rules 526 to 530 above shall be followed with the necessary changes in dealing with records in the record room (criminal section) of the District and Sessions Judge.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-chapter\"><h2>Chapter 21<br/>Inspection of Criminal Records by the Public</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">(The rules in this Chapter have been made under Section 554 of the Code)</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_532\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/100276611/\">532.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Subject to the rules hereinafter contained a legal practitioner entitled to practise in a Court may inspect the records of that Court and any party to a case or his recognized agent may inspect the record of that case whether pending or disposed of. Any other person desiring to inspect the record of a case, whether pending or decided, shall be required to state the purpose for which inspection is sought.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_533\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/97165123/\">533.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A book called the inspection book (in Form No. 131 on Schedule II-a) shall be kept by each Court and also by the record-keeper, and every person seeking inspection shall describe therein the record of which inspection is desired and note such other particulars as are necessary to show his title to inspect.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_534\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/41502328/\">534.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The records of all cases not deposited in the record room shall be open to inspection by order of the Presiding Judge or Magistrate, or during his absence, by order of the senior Judge or the senior magistrate at the station. The records deposited in the record room shall be open to inspection by order of the ministerial officer in charge of the office.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_535\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/22222142/\">535.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The inspection of records shall be made between such hours, in such place, and in the presence of such official as the Presiding Judge or Magistrate may order, provided that where the Magistrate is subordinate to the District Magistrate his order shall be subject to the District Magistrate's control.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_536\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/173004674/\">536.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Except as provided in Rule 540, an inspection fee of 12 annas an hour or fraction of an hour shall be charged for every record inspected.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_537\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/137075788/\">537.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Records shall not be removed from the custody of the Courts to which they pertain or from the record-room in which they are kept except-</span></span><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_537.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/28919458/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">by order of superior judicial authority;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_537.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/25018033/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">on the requisition of the Government, the Commissioner of the divisions, the Inspector-General of Police, the Magistrate of the District, or a Court, civil or criminal having occasion to refer to a record in the course of a trial;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_537.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/76118032/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">on the requisition of the head copyist for the preparation of the copies of pending records.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Facilities should accordingly be given by every Court for inspection in its own office of any record to which a public officer not entitled to call for records may wish to refer. When a public officer not entitled to call for records requires for official purposes a copy of any portion of a record kept in an office in the same station, the copy may be made in that office by any trustworthy person whom he may depute for the purpose. When the record is not in an office in the same station, the copy shall be made by the office in which it is kept and shall be sent to the office requiring it.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - The copy so made cannot, as it stands be used for judicial purposes until it is certified; but a copy so made can be sent to be certified by the officer in charge of the records from which it was made if it is one that would have been supplied free of charge had it been applied for under the provisions of Part V, Chapter 26, Rule 641.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_538\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/123382565/\">538.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Books and registers kept under the order of the High Court are open to inspection by the public. The fees shall be 6 annas an hour or fraction of an hour occupied in the inspection, irrespective of the nature or number of the books or registers inspected. Any person seeking inspection shall enter in the inspection book his name and occupation and particulars of the book or register of which inspection is sought.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_539\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/119348238/\">539.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Inspection fees shall be paid in court-stamps. The record- keeper or in a Court the official placed in charge of the book by the Presiding Judge or Magistrate, shall affix the stamps, in the column provided in the inspection book, and cancel them in the manner required by Section 30 of the Court-fees Act (VII of 1870).</span><span class=\"akn-p\">The Judge or Magistrate or the ministerial officer by whose orders the inspection is allowed shall see that the stamps are duly affixed and cancelled. The fees shall be prepaid and shall in no case be refunded.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_540\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/34649853/\">540.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No inspection fee shall be charged for the inspection of records, books and registers by Government law officers, or other persons duly authorized in this behalf, for Government purposes, for the inspection of the record of a pending case a party thereto or by his pleader or recognized agent or his pleader's recognized clerk, or for the inspection of a record by any one when the inspection is made at the request of the Court. The record of a pending case includes the record of a decided case called for in connection with a pending case. The inspection fee may be remitted by the Sessions Judge or the District Magistrate in the case of press correspondents who seek inspection of judgements or final orders with a view to publication in a newspaper. When inspection fees are remitted an entry to that effect shall be made in the column provided for affixing the Court-fee labels in the inspection book and the reason for remission shall be noted in the remarks column.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - The Public Prosecutor's clerk is deemed to be duly authorised to inspect the record of a case in which the Public Prosecutor appear for Government. With this exception the clerks of legal practitioners are not exempted by the above rule.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_541\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/100884092/\">541.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The use of pen and ink during inspection is prohibited. Pencil and paper may be used for making note or copies from the record, but no marks shall be made on any record or paper inspected. Any person infringing this rule may be deprived, by order of the Presiding Judge or Magistrate, of the right of inspection for such period as the Judge or Magistrate may direct. Such an order when passed by a Magistrate subordinate to the District Magistrate shall be subject to the latter's approval.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_542\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/76968771/\">542.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">It shall be the duty of the official supervising the inspection of a record to see that no alterations are made in it or papers abstracted, and that it is returned in its original condition when the inspection is over. He shall permit none but the applicant himself to inspect the record or to take notes or copies therefrom. The inspection shall ordinarily be completed and the record returned with the office hours of the day on which the record was taken out for examination.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_543\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/110167527/\">543.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If the applicant fails to make inspection within one week from the date on which inspection was sanctioned the order shall lapse and no further inspection shall be allowed without a fresh application.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_544\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/143461454/\">544.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When the record of a criminal case is given for inspection, the police case-diary and the translation thereof, if any, shall invariably be removed from the file. Parties and pleaders shall not be allowed access to these documents.</span></span></section></section></section><section class=\"akn-part\"><h2>Part III \u2013 Chapter 22</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Rules and Instructions Under the Court-Fees Act</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A. Court-fees Payable on Complaints</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_545\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/100002802/\">545.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_545.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/46564343/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Under Article 1 (b) of Schedule II of the Court-Fees Act 1870 (IX of 1870), a fee of [two rupees] <span class=\"akn-remark\" data-status=\"editorial\">[Substituted by M.P. 12 of 1966.]</span> is leviable on petition or application containing a complaint or charge of any offences other than an offence for which police officers may under the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898, arrest without warrant when presented to a Criminal Court.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_545.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/133868895/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Under Section 18 of the Court-fees Act a fee of eight annas is to be levied, unless the Court thinks fit to remit the payment, when a person is examined on a complaint and-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_545.2.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/83914335/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">a previous petition with Court-fee has not already been presented, and</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_545.2.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/79133861/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the offence complained of is a non-cognizablc one, or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_545.2.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/167423026/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the offence is wrongful restraint or wrongful confinement.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_545.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/41514736/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No fee is leviable under Article 1 (b) of Schedule II of the Court-fees Act on a complaint of any cognizable offence. No fee is leviable under Section 18 of the Court-fees Act in respect of a complaint of any cognizable offence other than wrongful restriaint or wrongful confinement.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B. Process-fees</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Rules under Section 20 (ii) of the Court-fees Act</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_546\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/52278238/\">546.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The following rules have been made under Section 20 (ii) of the Court-fees Act-</span></span><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/156449696/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The fees hereinafter mentioned shall be chargeable for serving and executing process issued by Criminal Courts in the case of offences other than offences for which police officers may arrest without a warrant-</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(1)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">For the issue of a summons to an accused person or witness, or for the issue of a notice to the opposite party in an appeal or revision, in respect of each person - Re. 0-12-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/16680304/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">For the issue of a warrant of arrest in respect of each person - Rs. 2-0-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/133502287/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In respect of proclamation for an absconding person under Section 87 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898 - Rs. 2-0-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/117042203/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">For warrant of attachment, in respect of each person - Rs. 1-8-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/90906565/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In cases where an application is made by a complainant for the recovery of fees ordered to be repaid under Section 31 of the Court-fees Act, 1870, or of fees ordered to be paid under Section 546-A of the Code of Criminal Procedure, or of compensation granted under Section 545 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898 or by an accused person for the recovery of compensation awarded to him under Section 250 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, 1898;</span><span class=\"akn-p\">For the issue of a warrant for the levy of fees, fines or compensation - Re. 1-0-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_546.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/74250838/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Notice injunction or any other process not otherwise provided for - Rs. 1-8-0.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(2)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No fees shall be chargeable for any process issued upon the complaint or application of any public officer as defined in Section 2 of the Code of Civil Procedure, 1908, when acting as such public officer, or of any railway servant as defined in Section 3 of the Railways Act, 1890 when acting as such railway servant.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">This exemption shall not, however, apply to cases instituted on complaint by a police officer authorized under the Central Provinces and Berar Municipalities Act, 1922 (II of 1922), or rules or bye-laws made thereunder.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(3)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No fee shall be chargeable for any process to compel the appearance of a witness recalled for cross-examination under the provisions of Section 256 of the Code of Criminal Procedure.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(4)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The presiding officer of the Court may remit in whole or in part any fee chargeable under sub-rule (1) of these rules whenever he is satisfied that the person applying for the issue of the process is unable to pay such fee.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_547\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/158558266/\">547.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Process-fee must be paid in court-fee stamps and not in cash. The stamps shall be affixed to an application or memorandum, as is appropriate filed in Court. The application or memorandum should include the description of the Court, the number of the case, the section and the Act under which the offence is punishable, the value of the Court-fee stamps affixed, details of the processes to be issued and full particulars and addresses of the persons on whom the processes are to be served. If an application is filed it must in addition to the requisite stamps for the process-fees bear such stamps as are necessary for its own validity. No process for the issue of which payment of a fee is required shall be drawn up until the fee has been paid.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Courts appear to find difficulty in dealing with the filing of applications and the Court-fees payable on them. The general rule is that an application or petition to a Criminal Court, unless otherwise provided, requires a Court fee stamp under Article 1 Schedule II of the Court fees Act. For certain purposes the Code of Criminal Procedure requires an application to the Court precedent to action being taken. For other purposes the presiding officer may require an application to be filed. On other cases an application is neither necessary nor compellable and the Court is required to proceed of its own month. It is the duty of the presiding officer to see that applications are filed where necessary, i.e. when the Code requires an application and that all applications which require Court-fee stamps are properly stamped. The principle may be explained by reference to the two following examples-</span></span><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_547.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/38753697/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Section 244 (2) of the Code provides that a Magistrate trying a summons case may on the application of the complainant or accused issue summons to a witness. For this purpose therefore it is necessary to require an application. Such an application would require to be stamped under Article 1 of Schedule II of the Court-fee Act unless it were an application of the type referred to in clause (xiv) of Section 19 of the Court-fees Act.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_547.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/128754174/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Section 252 (2) of the Code provides that in trying a warrant case the Magistrate shall ascertain the names of persons likely to be acquainted with the facts of the case and shall summons such as he deems necessary. In such a case therefore the Magistrate cannot compel the filing of an application praying for the summoning of witnesses. If, however, the complainant elects to file an application for this purposes the Magistrate must see that it is properly stamped.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_548\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/93617246/\">548.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No fee can be charged for the issue of process in a congnizabie case whether instituted on complaint or not. The question whether fees are chargeable in any particular case should be determined by the Magistrate with reference to the section of the Indian Penal Code or other law relating to the offence in respect of which he directs process to issue, whatever the section or law may be that is quoted in the complaint.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_549\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/128837737/\">549.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A table in English and in the language of the Court showing the fees chargeable for the issue of processes and stating that process-fees are to be paid in Court-fee stamps and not in cash shall be exhibited in a conspicuous part of each Court-room.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Remissions of Court-fees made by the provincial Government under Section 35 of the Court-fees Act</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_550\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/35579705/\">550.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">So far as Criminal Courts are concerned, the following remissions are made by the Provincial Government in Court-fees chargeable under the First and Second Schedules of Court-fees Act, 1870:-</span></span><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_550.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/85197299/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If the amount of the fee chargeable in any case involves a fraction of an anna the fraction shall be remitted, except where otherwise expressly provided for.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">*               *               *</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_550.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a the executants.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">*               *               *</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_550.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/28555188/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The fees chargeable under Articles 6,7 and 9 of the First Schedule on copies furnished by...... Criminal Courts....... for the private use of persons applying for them:</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Provided that nothing in this clause shall apply to copies when filed exhibited or recorded in any namely:-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_550.13.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/136514369/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">copy              *</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_550.36\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/93800238/\">(36)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span
