class=\"akn-p\">Abstract of the register of miscellaneous proceedings</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">V-49</span></td>\n</tr>\n<tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">8.</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Appeal and revision abstracts</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">V-52 and 53</span></td>\n</tr>\n<tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">9.</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Abstract of fine accounts</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">V-54</span></td>\n</tr>\n<tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">10.</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Statement of fines paid into and refunded from the treasury</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">V-61.</span></td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table></div></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_594\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/63766694/\">594.</a> Calendars.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- Calendars are to be submitted to the District Magistrate by each subordinate court. The daily calendar will be submitted for all cases tried regularly and in proceedings under Chapter VIII of the Code of Criminal Procedure. The weekly calendar will be submitted for cases tried summarily in which either-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_594.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/107993372/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the accused had to appear on more than two hearings, no matter whether the cases ended in conviction or acquittal or discharge, or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_594.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/114001203/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">there was a conviction resulting otherwise than in a fine not exceeding Rs. 5.</span></span></section><span class=\"akn-wrapUp\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If the Court is immediately subordinate to a Sub-Divisional Magistrate stationed at a place other than the headquarters of the district is shall be submitted through the Sub-Divisional Magistrate. District Magistrates shall forward their own calendars to the Sessions Judge. They shall also forward to the Sessions Judge calendars of Magistrates noting what action has been taken on them. In cases submitted under Section 349 of the Code of Criminal Procedure, hereinafter called \"the Code\", to a Sub-Divisional Magistrate the latter shall enter his own proceedings on the calendar submitted by the first Court so that the whole course of the trial may be seen in one statement.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_595\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/101477246/\">595.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">After scrutiny calendars shall be returned through the channels by which they were submitted to the Court which prepared them. The calendar for the year shall be preserved for one year and then destroyed.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_596\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/129828300/\">596.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Calendars help District Magistrates and Sessions Judges to maintain constant supervision over Subordinate Courts and to discover irregularities which require to be checked or reported under Section 438 of the Code. In addition to matters indicated in Part I of this volume as requiring scrutiny the following are matters to which scrutiny should especially be directed:-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_596.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/183795047/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Duration - When the duration of a State case tried regularly exceeds 30 days or of a complaint case 45 days an explanation of the delay shall be entered in the daily calendar by the Magistrate. When in a case tried summarily an accused has had to appear more than twice an explanation shall be entered in the weekly calendar.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_596.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/173249757/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Treatment of habitual prisoners - When an accused is liable to enhanced punishment an explanation shall be recorded if such punishment is not awarded.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_596.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/101902393/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The proper use of Sections 545 and 546-A of the Code.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_596.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/36432071/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Sentence - The sentence imposed in summary cases as entered in the weekly calendar should be scrutinized with the same care as the sentence imposed in regular cases entered in the daily-calendar.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_597\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/183670955/\">597.</a> Statistical sheet.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/197163376/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The particulars of all original cases, security proceedings under Chapter VIII and commitment enquiries under Chapter XVIII of the Code shall be entered in this sheet by the Court Moharrir as each case is disposed of. The term \"disposed of' includes transfer to another province, commitment to a Court of Session or reference to a superior court for final orders on proceedings already held, e.g., under Section 123, 349 or 562 of the Code or under Section 9 or 31 of the Reformatory Schools Act, 1897, or under Section 5 or 6 of the Central Provinces Borstal Act, 1928, or under Section 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act, 1936 but does not include transfer to another court within the province or submission to a superior Court e.g., under Section 346 of the Code with a view to the trial being held de novo.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/139097240/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A single sheet may include the statistics of several cases. When a case which has been referred to a superior Court for final orders on proceedings already held is disposed of, the entries in the sheet prepared by the reader of the Court receiving the reference shall be made in red ink.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/165624733/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When an accused person is tried at one trial under Section 234 of the Code on charges of distinct offences, each supported by separate and independent evidence, the number of such offences shall be entered in column 4. But when an accused person is tried at one trial under Section 335 of the Code for several offences arising out of the same transaction or on alternative charges under Section 336, the figure I shall be entered in column 4 and only the principal offence of which the accused is convicted (or, in case of acquittal, the principal offences of with which he is charged) shall be entered in column 2. In doubtful cases the orders of the Magistrate should be taken as to which of the several offences should be deemed to be the principal offence. The columns showing persons brought for trial and persons disposed of are to be filled in on similar principles. An accused person is said to be brought to trial when he is produced or when he appears personally or by agent before the Court. The following examples are appended for guidance.</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.3.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/16275892/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A is charged with and tried at one trial for three thefts committed within the space of twelve months. He is convicted on two charges and acquitted on the third charge. The sheet should show three cases brought to trial (column 4), three persons brought to trial (column 9), one person acquitted (column 11), and two persons convicted (column 12).</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.3.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/111909981/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A is charged with and tried at one trial under Section 235 of the Code for the offences of rioting, voluntarily causing grievous hurt and assaulting a public servant endevouring in the discharge of his duty to suppress the riot, all the acts being so connected together as to form the same transaction. A is acquitted of the offence under Section 147 of the Indian Penal Code, but is convicted of offences under Sections 152 and 325 and is sentenced to a term of imprisonment for each offences. The sheet should show one case and one person brought to trial under Section 325 (columns 2, 4 and 9) and one person convicted (column 12), the acquittal under Section 147 and the conviction under Section 152 being left out of account.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.3.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/67430364/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A is charged with and convicted in the alternative of theft in a building or receiving stolen property. For statistical purposes only the former offence should be taken into account.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/45847916/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where several persons are tried jointly at one trial under Section 325 of the Code, the principles given in sub-rule (3) above should be followed, and only the major offences shall be reported for the purposes of the statistical sheet. An example is given below:-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Nine accused are tried jointly; two are discharged, seven are charged under Section 147/325 of the Penal Code: of these seven, six are convicted under Section 147 and Section 325 and given separate sentences under each section, and one is convicted under Section 323.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">The statistical sheet will show Section 325 and Section 323 as the law applicable (column 2) and against each section there will appear a line of entries. Against Section 325 the entries will be one case brought to trial (column 4) and one case disposed of (column 6); the number of persons brought to trial will be eight (column 9), two discharged (column 11) and six convicted (column 12). The number of cases will be one (column 20). The remarks column will refer to column 9 and say \"Excludes one person convicted under Section 323, Indian Penal Code\".</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Against Section 325 (column 2) there will be no entry in columns 4 and 6, and the only entries will be one person brought to trial (column 9), one person convicted (column 12), and in the remarks column a reference to column 9 saying \"include the person mentioned above\", i.e., in the remarks column of the line of entries against Section 325.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/167974568/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In column 3 shall be entered all those cases is which during the year a magistrate declared that the charge was false or that the facts alleged did not amount to an offence or that the offence never occurred. Cases in which action was taken under Section 250 of the Code and the complainant was ordered to pay compensation shall be included. When a complaint against a number of persons is found to be false against some and true against others it shall be regarded as a true case.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/17474869/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When an accused person, subject to military laws, is transferred from a Magistrate's Court before which he was brought to trial to the military authorities for trial by court-martial, the transfer is to be considered as a transfer to another province and shown accordingly in column 15 of the sheet.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/91891102/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">An accused person, in respect of whom an order is made dismissing the case or releasing the offender, either unconditionally or conditionally on his executing a bond, under Section 4 or Section 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act, 1936, shall, notwithstanding that the Court has not proceeded to conviction, be shown in column 12 of the sheet and a corresponding entry made in column 16. A note should be made in the remarks column in respect of the persons entered for statistical purposes as convicted but in fact dealt with under Section 4 (1) (i) of the Act and not convicted.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.8\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/19726340/\">(8)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In column 16 shall be entered cases dealt with under Section 562 of the Code, Section 31 of the Reformatory Schools Act, 1897, Section 28 of the Central Provinces Children Act, 1928, Section 3 or 4 or 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act, 1936, Section 130 of the Railways Act, 1930, and any similar enactment which permits the release of an offender without the imposition of a substantive sentence of imprisonment, fine, whipping or detention.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.9\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/6156861/\">(9)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In column 19 shall be noted the number of persons convicted of offence under Chapter XII or Chapter XVIII of the Indian Penal Code and liable to enhanced punishment under Section 75 of that Code on account of their previous convictions, whether or not such enhanced punishment was actually awarded.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.10\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/45731199/\">(10)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Cases in which an accused person has been forwarded in custody or on bail to the magistrate, after authorized investigation by police officers, revenue officers or other Courts are designated State cases. Cases of which cognizance is taken under Section 190 (1) (a) or (c) of the Code or designated complaint cases.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.11\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/13406978/\">(11)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Both in State cases and in complaint cases duration shall be calculated from the date of the apprehension of the accused or from the date of his appearance in Court, whichever is earlier. When a case which has not been disposed of within the meaning of sub-rule (1) is received by another Court, duration shall be calculated from the date of apprehension or appearance in the first Court. In cases having more accused persons than one, duration shall be calculated from the earliest date on which any accused appeared in court or was apprehended.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_597.12\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/118207455/\">(12)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A note shall be made in the remarks column of that sheet-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/172550972/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of an accused being required to keep the peace under Section 106 of the Code;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/26508177/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of an accused being a male juvenile;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/104573072/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of an accused who is a male juvenile being sentenced to whipping;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/21563422/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of any complainant being ordered to pay compensation under Section 250 of the Code, the number of accused persons affected being stated;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.e\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/71075901/\">(e)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of detail regarding the persons returned in column 15;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.f\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/189826094/\">(f)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of previous convicts shown in column 19, who were ordered to notify their residence to the police after their release or who were sentenced to suffer solitary confinement;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.g\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/148405351/\">(g)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of the fact that the entries relate to the retrial of, or further enquiry into a case once decided which has been ordered by an Appellate or Revisional Court, by writing the word retrial in red ink;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.h\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/64087602/\">(h)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of an accused shown as convicted in column 12 in respect of whom the Court has not proceeded to conviction under Section 4 or Section 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act, 1936;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_597.12.i\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/149611155/\">(i)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">of the various enactments under which persons returned in column 16 have been dealt with.</span></span></section></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_598\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/66221418/\">598.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The statistical sheet shall ordinarily accompany the daily dispatch of records to the statistical writer on their way to the record room. When for any reason a record cannot be sent at once to the record-keeper a note to that effect shall be made in the statistical sheet and the latter shall be sent to the statistical writer unaccompanied by the record.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_599\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/106529385/\">599.</a> Witness memorandum.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_599.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/122376176/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When the first witness in a case appears the headings in the form shall be filled in and his attendance noted, particulars as to other witnesses shall be filled in regularly as they attend, receive diet-money, and are discharged from attendance.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_599.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/163303254/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">For the purposes of column 5 a witness shall be regarded as in attendance on every day on which he is actually present in Court even though the case is not called up for hearing on any such day.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_599.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/124746125/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A witness shall not be regarded as finally discharged from attendance if he is allowed to leave the Court, under orders to attend again in the same court in the same case. When any witness who has been discharged is resummoned for coss-examination under the provisions of Section 257 of the Code, the necessary additions shall be made in columns 3,4 and 8 of the memorandum.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_599.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/56105460/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Witnesses examined in preliminary enquiries under Sections 202 and 476 of the Code need not be entered in the memorandum.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_599.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/105055723/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When the hearing in the Court is concluded, columns 5 to 8 shall be totalled and the memorandum placed before the Presiding Officer, who after satisfying himself that all the entries have been correctly made shall sign it and have it filed with the record. When the case is committed for trial, or referred under Section 123 of the Code, to the Code of Session, the memorandum shall be sent direct to the statistical clerk, who shall file it with the record on its receipt from the Court of Session.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_600\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/137613830/\">600.</a> List of complaints rejected.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- Entries in this list shall be made as soon as possible after each complaint is dismissed.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_601\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/5952640/\">601.</a> Memorandum of pending cases.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- All cases pending at the end of the year shall be entered in this memorandum. If the case has not then been brought for trial, the entry in column 6 shall be nil. A note similar to that prescribed in Rule 597 (12) (g) shall be made against each line of entries relation to a case of retrial or further enquiry.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_602\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/22737933/\">602.</a> Abstract of the register of miscellaneous proceedings.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- At the close of the year the contents of the register of miscellaneous proceedings so far as they relate to cases under the Code, shall be abstracted in the form used for Statement III referred to in Rule 607 by the reader of each court and sent to the statistical clerk. No statistics are required of cases under other laws. Cases referred under Section 123 of the Code should not be shown in column 4 as \"pending\" but in the remarks column a note shall be added, namely, \"referred under Section 123 of the Code\".</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_603\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/182164742/\">603.</a> Appeal and revision abstracts.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_603.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/46998258/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">At the close of the year reader of each Court invested with appellate powers shall prepare an abstract of the contents of the appeal and revision registers in forms similar to Statements VI-A and VI-B. The figures for the several classes of Court from which appeals are heard shall be separately grouped and totaled as follows :-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_603.1.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/5653596/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Special Magistrates appointed under Section 14 of the Code.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_603.1.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/6463324/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Stipendiary Magistrates sitting singly.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_603.1.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/83638589/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Honorary Magistrates sitting singly.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_603.1.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/5041979/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Benches of honorary Magistrates.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_603.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/153823538/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Only those persons who are entered in column 4 of the revision register shall be shown in columns 2 and 3 of the revision abstract. The number of complainants entered in column 3 of the register, along with the number of accused persons affected by their application, shall be noted in the remarks column of the abstract; those accused persons though not appearing in column 2 or 3, shall be shown in their proper places in columns 5 to 12 according to the result of the applications affecting them.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_603.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/111415526/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The number of convicted persons required to keep the peace under Section 106 (3) of the Code and the number of youthful offenders sent to a reformatory school or to a Borstal institution by Courts of appeal shall ne entered in the remarks column. No entry shall be made in column 14 of the abstracts when a sole appellant or sole applicant dies or escapes or his case is transferred to another province.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_604\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/131564484/\">604.</a> Abstract of fine accounts.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- The reader of each Magistrate's Court shall at the end of each month prepare an abstract of the fine accounts of his court is the form of Statement VII. Fines imposed by a Court in the exercise of appellate jurisdiction shall not be shown in the abstract. Fines imposed in cases received on reference from an inferior court shall be shown separately in red ink. The amounts shall be given to the nearest rupee. The statistical clerk shall compile these abstracts and submit them to the District Magistrate who after scrutinizing them shall issue such instructions in the matter of recovery and credit of fines as may appear necessary.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_605\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/28476002/\">605.</a> Statement of fines credited into the treasury.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- The moharrir shall at the end of each month prepare in the form bearing serial No. 61, on Schedule V-Criminal Judicial English, a statement of all fines credited into the treasury under the Major Head XXI. - Administration of Justice. The amounts of fines held in revenue deposits for subsequent payment to parties shall not be included in this statement. To facilitate the payment of grant-in aid to local bodies under the Central Provinces and Berar Local Bodies Act, 1939, the statement shall show in a group separate from the group in which the rest of the fines credited into the treasury are shown, all fines referred to in column (2) of the list printed at the end of Rule 365. The moharrir shall also prepare at the end of each month a statement of refunds of fines referred to in column (2) of the aforementioned list.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_606\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/17218158/\">606.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The two statements shall be checked by the Magistrate with the figure in the Fine Register. The Magistrate shall then endorse on each statement a certificate signed by him the effect that the figures in the statement have been checked with the entries in the Fine Register and found to be correct. The statements shall then be forwarded to the District Magistrate.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_607\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/68399114/\">607.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The following statements shall be submitted annually by the District Magistrate through the Sessions Judge to the High Court in the forms and on the dates shown against them :-</span><div class=\"akn--table-container\"><table class=\"akn-table\" data-eid=\"att_1__part_IV__chp_25__sec_607__table_1\" id=\"att_1__part_IV__chp_25__sec_607__table_1\">\n<tbody><tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Name of return</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No. of form on Schedule</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Date of dispatch</span></td>\n</tr>\n<tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">by District Magistrate to Sessions Judge</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">by Sessions Judge to the High Court</span></td>\n</tr>\n<tr class=\"akn-tr\">\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">I.-Tribunal statement</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">... V-55</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">...</span></td>\n<td class=\"akn-td\"><span class=\"akn-p\">...</span></td>\n</tr>\n</tbody></table></div></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_608\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/27691909/\">608.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">For the purpose of compiling the above statements the statistical clerk shall maintain the following ledgers:-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A. - Offence ledger (V-31).</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B. - Trial and duration ledger (V-32).</span><span class=\"akn-p\">C. - Punishment ledger (V-33).</span><span class=\"akn-p\">D. - Witness ledger (V-34).</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Instructions regarding the maintenance of these ledgers and the preparation of the statements are given below.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_609\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/154365887/\">609.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Only those cases for which statistical sheets are prepared under Rule 597 shall be included in the ledgers and the corresponding statements. The information given in the notes made in the statistical sheets shall be incorporated in the legders. In Ledger A separate pages shall be set apart for each side-head of crime as detailed in Statement II and in Ledgers B, C and D for each Court. The number of pages allotted should be sufficient to last for the calendar year. When a Magistrate is appointed to a district to replace a Magistrate who is transferred, his work shall be shown in that portion of the ledgers allotted to his predecessors. the names of only those Magistrates who are holding office at the end of the year shall be entered in the statements. The work of a Magistrate who is transferred during the year shall be shown against the name of his successor.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_610\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/149148445/\">610.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Figures relating to proceedings in a superior Court in cases referred to it for higher punishment or for final orders shall be shown in Statements IV, V, VII and VIII against the Court receiving the reference in red ink in a separate line below the black ink figures relating to that Court.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_611\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/76509784/\">611.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where further enquiry into a case, or retrial of or commitment for trial of a case which has once been decided, is ordered by an Appellate or Revisional Court, no entry regarding such further enquiry, retrial or commitment for trial shall be made in columns 5 to 8 of Ledger A or in columns 4 to 8 of Statement II. For all other purposes such further enquiry, retrial or commitment for trial shall be regarded as a fresh case.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_612\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/136912646/\">612.</a> Offence Ledger.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/55198454/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The figures for column 6 of this ledger are obtained from the list of complaints rejected and for the other columns from the statistical sheets and the memoranda of pending cases. On receipt of a record the statistical clerk shall see that no fresh entry is made in column 5 of the ledger of any case which was pending at the end of the previous year and which was therefore entered in the returns for that year. Similarly, no entry shall be made in column 9, if the accused has already been shown as brought to trial.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/107803336/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Column 9 shall include all cases brought to trial during the year, i.e., all cases in which the accused made his first appearance (personally or by agent) in the course of the year whether such cases are true or false and whether they were instituted during the year or were pending at the close of the previous year.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/136766757/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where an order is made under Section 4 or 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act dismissing the case or releasing the offender, either conditionally on his executing a bond or unconditionally, the case, notwithstanding that the Court has not proceeded to conviction, shall be entered in column 12. A note shall be made in the remarks column in respect of persons entered for statistical convenience as convicted, but in fact dealt with under Section 4 (1) (i) of the Act.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/170075196/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Details of compensation ordered to be paid under Section 250 of the Code and details regarding the persons shown in column 14 of the ledger shall be noted in the remarks column.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/64402383/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A note shall be made in the remarks column of the number of cases and the number of persons involved therein referred under Section 6 (1) of the Central Provinces Borstal Act.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_612.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/151978643/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Entries in the Offence Ledger for the case mentioned in Rule 597 (4) above should be made as follows: the side-head for Section 325 is No. 33: Section 325 of the Indian Penal Code will be entered in column 1, and against it will be shown one case reported during the year (column 5), one case found true (column 8) and one case brought to trial (column 9); two persons shall be shown as otherwise discharged (column 11) and six convicted (column 12), making a total of eight persons tried (column 15). In the remarks column there will be a reference to column 12 and the remarks \"Excludes one person transferred to side-head 34.\"</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Below this line of entries will be written \"Side-head 34\" and below it the following line of entries : Section 323 of the Indian Penal Code (column 1), one person convicted (column 12) and one persons tried (column 15). The remarks column will contain the remarks, referring to column 12, \"One person received from side-head 33\".</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_613\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/90071103/\">613.</a> Trial and duration ledger.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/156707212/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The figures for this ledger are obtained from the statistical sheets and from the memoranda of pending cases.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/98896581/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Cases in which a sole accused died, escaped or was transferred to another province, or was dealt with under Section 466 of the Code, shall be omitted from column 4 to 6,16 and 18.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/113661168/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Column 7 shall include all persons shown as pending at the end of the previous year after having been brought to trial during that year.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/97766365/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where an order is made under Section 4 or 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act dismissing the case or releasing the offender, either conditionally on his executing a bond or unconditionally, the case notwithstanding that the Court has not proceeded to conviction, shall be returned in column 12. A note shall be made in the remarks column in respect of persons entered for statistical purposes as convicted, but in fact dealt with under Section 4 (1) (i) of the Act and not convicted.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/50050328/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Persons whose cases are referred to a superior Court for final orders shall be entered in column 13 and not in columns 10 and 12 under the court making the reference. Under the Court receiving the reference, they shall be shown in red ink as convicted or acquitted according to the orders passed by it, or as pending if orders have not been passed.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/176374644/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The cases, of persons transferred from one Court to another Court within the provinces shall be entered only under the Court by which they are decided or in which they are pending at the end of the year if not decided.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/161441177/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A note shall be made in the remarks column of an accused person being a male juvenile and of details regarding the person shown in column 14 of the ledger.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_613.8\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/154432529/\">(8)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In the case given in rule 597(4) above the ledger will be filled up as follows: Nine persons will be shown as brought to trial (column 8) and two as otherwise discharged (column 11) making nine persons disposed of (column 15), and one State case (column 16).</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_614\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/22881711/\">614.</a> Punishment ledger.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/45896282/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The figures for columns 22 to 25 for this ledger are obtained from the statistical sheets and the figures for the other columns from the records. In column 22 shall be entered all persons entered in column 16 of the statistical sheet.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/102139084/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where an order is made under Section 4 or 5 of the Central Provinces Probation of Offenders Act dismissing the case or releasing the offender, either conditionally on his executing a bond or unconditionally, the case, notwithstanding that the Court has not proceeded to conviction shall be returned in column 22. A note shall be made in the remarks column both of the ledger and also of the Punishment Statement in respect of the persons entered for statistical convenience as convicted but in fact dealt under Section 4 (1) (i) of the Act and not convicted.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/185611152/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Where two penalties are inflicted on the same accused, each penalty shall be entered, in the appropriate column. Thus, a sentence of four months' simple imprisonment and fine of Rs. 15 requires until entries in columns 6,7,13 and 18. A sentence of one year's rigorous imprisonment with solitary confinement and whipping shall be noted in columns 4, 9 and 19. If an accused person is rigorously imprisoned for one year in default of giving security for goo behavior under Section 110 of the Code unit entries shall be made in columns 10, 11 and 19. The only exception to the rule is that when sentence of imprisonment or transportation are ordered to run concurrently one sentence shall be shown. The total of columns 4, 5, 6 and 11 should correspond with the total of columns 17 to 21, and the total of columns 7 and 8 with the total of columns 12 to 16.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/148603080/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">As regards persons whose cases have been referred for higher punishment for orders under Section 562 of the Code, or for confirmation of sentence, the punishment, if any, awarded by the superior Court shall be entered in red ink against such Court and not against the Court making the reference.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/13156730/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Only a forfeiture of property ordered as a substantive punishment under Section 126 or 127 of the Indian Penal Code shall be shown in columns 7 and 8, a note being made in the remarks column: confiscation of property, e.g., under the Excise Act, shall not be shown in the ledger.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/70315482/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When an offender has been sentenced to imprisonment and the sentence has been committed to one of detention in a reformatory school the sentence of imprisonment as well as the order for detention shall be shown in the appropriate column. But when an offender has been convicted and has in lieu of a sentence of transportation or imprisonment been ordered to be detained in a Borstal institution only the order of detention shall be shown.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/78583967/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The number of accused persons convicted of offences under Chapter XII or Chapter XVII of the Indian Penal Code, and liable to enhanced punishment under Section 75 ibid, shall be shown in column 25. A note shall be made in the remarks column of any person ordered to suffer solitary confinement or to notify his residence to the police after release from jail in addition to the primary sentence.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.8\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/69854635/\">(8)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When a convicted person is required to keep the peace under Section 106 of the Code, the fact shall be noted in the remarks column.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_614.9\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/58370737/\">(9)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In the case given in rule 597 (4) above the ledger will show the details of the punishment awarded to seven persons in accordance with the instructions in this rule.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_615\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/152534206/\">615.</a> Witness ledger.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- the figures for this ledger are obtained from the witness memoranda. The number of witnesses, if any, examined by a Court to which a case is referred shall be shown under the Court in red ink.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_616\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/196605712/\">616.</a> Tribunal statement.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- The preparation of this statement presents no difficulty. Column 9 showing the total number of cases disposed of during the year should correspond with column 6 of Statement IV including the number of referred cases entered in that column in red ink. The figure for column 10 is the same as the figure shown in column 3 of Statement III against side-head 2.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_617\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/89402772/\">617.</a> Offence statement.</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/3915732/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The figures for this statement are obtained from Ledger A.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/36279047/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In compiling the statement the printed schedule of offences shall be adhered to. The list offences under special and local laws is not exhaustive : additional entries shall be made in alphabetical order of each law against which offences were alleged to have been committed. Abetments and attempts, where not separately specified in the schedule, shall be included with the substantive offences abetted or attempted.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/165027829/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The entries in columns 4,7 and 9 of the statement shall not include any cases already shown in the corresponding columns for the previous year. No case which are pending shall be shown in column 7.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.4\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/143375788/\">(4)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Details of persons in column 15 of the statement shall be given in the remarks column against the persons shown in that column as in the offence ledger.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.5\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/112284990/\">(5)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The number of complainants ordered to pay compensation and the number of accused to whom it was paid shall be noted in the remarks column against each side-head in a case under which such action was taken.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.6\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/60888754/\">(6)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A note shall be made in the statement corresponding to the note required in rule 614(4) against the Offence Ledger.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_617.7\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/50238824/\">(7)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In the case given in Rule 597 (4) above the statement will be drawn up as follows : Against side-head 21 there will be one offence reported (column 4), one brought to trial (column 9); eight persons under trial (column 10), two persons acquitted or discharged (column 12) and six persons convicted (column 13). Against side-head 22 there will be one person under trial (column 10) and one convicted (column 13), and no entries in columns 3 to 9 inclusive.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_618\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/121062288/\">618.</a> Statement of miscellaneous proceedings.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- This statement is prepared from the abstracts of the register of miscellaneous proceedings furnished by readers under Rule 602.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_619\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/19778427/\">619.</a> Trial and duration statement.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- This statement is compiled from Ledger B. The figures for the several classes of Courts in column 1 shall be separately grouped and totalled as follows:-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_619.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/13279593/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Special Magistrates appointed under Section 14 of the Code.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_619.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/11154591/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Chief Magistrate of the district.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_619.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/189481758/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Stipendiary Magistrates sitting singly.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_619.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/152778434/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Honorary Magistrates sitting singly.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_619.e\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/147341259/\">(e)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Benches of honorary Magistrates.</span></span></section><span class=\"akn-wrapUp\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The total number of male juveniles tried during the year and details of the persons shown in column 16 shall be given in the remarks column.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_620\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/130495725/\">620.</a> Punishment statement.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- This statement is complied from Ledger C. The figures shall be grouped and totalled as in Statement IV. The total number of convicted persons required to keep the peace under Section 106 of the Code and of those dealt with under Section 130 of the Indian Railways Act, 1890, by ordering the parent or guardian to execute a bond shall be shown in the remarks column.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_621\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/92945515/\">621.</a> Appeal and revision statement.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- These statements are prepared from the appeal and revision abstract furnished by readers under rule 608. The figures relating to each Appellate Court shall be grouped together and totalled separately. The grand total for the district shall be given at the foot of the statement.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_622\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/132598122/\">622.</a> Fine account.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- This statement is prepared from the abstracts of fine accounts received from readers under Rule 604. The Courts shall be grouped as in Statement IV.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_623\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/70904332/\">623.</a> Witness statement.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- This statement is compiled from Ledger D. The Courts shall be grouped as in Statement IV.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_624\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/4594283/\">624.</a> Report of offences against the coinage.</h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">- If an unusual number of counterfeit coins is received in any Court a special report shall be submitted to the High Court in order that the fact may be brought to the notice of the executive authorities.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_625\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/41255684/\">625.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In order to expedite the compilation of provincial returns advance copies of all the annual statement shall be sent direct to the High Court simultaneously with the dispatch of the annual report and statements to the Sessions Judge. When a Sessions Judge finds it necessary to address a District Magistrate with regard to the correctness of the figures in these statements a copy of the letter shall be sent to the High Court, and the District Magistrate shall send to the High Court a copy of his reply.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B.-Sessions Court Returns</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_626\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/116819591/\">626.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The following returns shall be submitted by Sessions Judges to the High Court in
