for inspection of Court and other registers.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_751\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/165505266/\">751.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_751.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/103005917/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every application for recognition shall be made by a legal practitioner, by a letter addressed to the District Judge in the following form:-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">\"I beg that (name)............ son of.......... aged....... resident of........... may be recognized as my clerk.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">I have made due enquiries with regard to the character and qualifications of the candidate, and certify that in my opinion he is a fit and proper person to be recognized as a legal practitioner's clerk, under the rules made by the High Court of Judicature at Nagpur. I also certify that he will be employed bona fide in my service for clerical work\".</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_751.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/104474274/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The application shall State the legal practitioner's standing at the Bar, the name or names of the recognized clerks, if any, already in his service, and the educational qualifications of the person proposed to be employed as a recognized clerk.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_752\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/53479694/\">752.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">An application for renewal of recognition shall be made by the legal practitioner to the District Judge before the 15th January of each year.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_753\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/12190608/\">753.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A fee of Re. 1 for recognition and an annual fee of Re. 1 for the renewal of recognition shall be payable in respect of each clerk. the fee payable for renewal will be Rs. 2, if the application for renewal is made after the date mentioned in Rule 752. These fees shall be paid in the shape of court-fee stamps affixed to the applications.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_754\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/108471441/\">754.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No person convicted of an offence involving moral turpitude shall be registered as a recognized clerk, unless after taking into consideration the age and antecedents of the persons, the circumstances in which the offence was committed, the interval since conviction, and the conduct of the person during that interval, the District Judge is of the opinion that the conviction should no longer operate as a bar to registration. No person shall be registered as a recognized clerk unless he is approved by the Bar Association, and unless the District Judge is satisfied that he has had a sufficient elementary education in the language of the district, Hindi or Marathi, and also in English if the legal practitioner employing him is practising in the High Court.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_755\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/154281160/\">755.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No person shall be admitted or continued as a recognized clerk if he is, or acts as, a recognized agent (mukhtyar), either under a special or general power of attorney, or any person other than the legal practitioner by whom he is employed.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_756\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/164908493/\">756.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The names with necessary particulars of recognized clerks registered in the office of a District Judge shall be intimated to subordinate Courts and the District Magistrate. On receipt of the information the Judge or the senior judge, as the case may be, at outlying stations shall have the necessary entries made in the register, which shall be maintained in the form given in Rule 750.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_757\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/180408105/\">757.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No clerk recognised as the clerk of one legal practitioner shall do business in Courts or in offices thereof on behalf of any other legal practitioner unless permitted in writing to do so by his master on special occasions.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Two legal practitioners shall not be allowed to engage the same clerk, provided that if the two legal practitioners are closely related, such as father and son or brothers, they may be allowed to have one clerk.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_758\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/121105047/\">758.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No clerk employed by a legal practitioner shall be allowed access to the High Court or any court subordinate to it, or to any of the offices attached thereto, unless he is a recognized clerk.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_759\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/128617780/\">759.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_759.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/79804045/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A registered clerk may act in all matter of a routine nature which do not require the personal attendance of legal practitioners such as-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_759.1.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/112556663/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">to present applications signed by his master for-</span></span><section class=\"akn-subparagraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(i)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">copies of records,</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subparagraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(ii)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">return of documents,</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subparagraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(iii)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">issue of process with diet-money, if any,</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subparagraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(iv)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">payment of incidental costs,</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subparagraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(v)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">translation and typing of evidence in the High Court;</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_759.1.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/36581668/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">to inspect records, if authorized by his master and sanctioned by the Court or other officer empowered to do so;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_759.1.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/3585208/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">to file powers of attorney in favour of his master;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_759.1.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/54632229/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">to identify, if required, and if in a position to do so, persons making inspection of records or swearing affidavits.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_759.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/103790483/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Acts which the law requires to be done by a party or his recognized agent or by pleader duly appointed on his behalf, such as the presentation of a plaint or memorandum of appeal, shall not be done by a recognized clerk.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_759.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/55610329/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">When a recognized clerk receives any money from his master's employer he shall give to the employer a receipt for the amount received by him specifying exactly what the money was received for, e.g., writing fees or costs, and if for costs, for what costs, e.g., plaint, process-fees, pleader's fee, etc. the details shall be set out separately either in the receipt itself, or on a separate piece of paper attached to it.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_760\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/87585207/\">760.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The District Judge, for reasons to be recorded in writing, and after hearing the clerk in his defence, if he so desires, may order the removal of any recognized clerk and strike off his name from the register, and on the passing of such order the clerk shall cease to be a recognized clerk. Every such order shall be communicated to all concerned as in Rule 756.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Note. - Proceedings taken against clerks under this rule are administrative and not judicial proceedings.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_761\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/169246269/\">761.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No person removed under the preceding rule shall be recommended for registration by any legal practitioner at the same or at any other station unless he has been declared to be eligible for registration under Rule 763.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_762\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/139547385/\">762.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The name of a recognized clerk found on enquiry under Rule 760 to be using the Court premises, for private purposes, such as preparation of documents unconnected with any case in which his master is engaged, may be struck off from the register.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_763\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/7401683/\">763.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The District Judge may at any time revise an order passed by him under Rule 760 and may, for reasons to be recorded in writing, reinstate the person removed or declared him eligible for registration.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_764\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/167077281/\">764.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Whenever a pleader ceases to employ a recognized clerk he shall notify the fact to the District Judge and shall also briefly state the reason why he has ceased to employ him. On receipt of this information the name of the clerk shall be struck off the register and all concerned shall be informed as in Rule 756.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-chapter\"><h2>Chapter 39<br/>Petition-Writers</h2>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The following rules regarding petition-writers have been made by the High Court under Section 28-A of the Central Provinces Courts Act, 1917, as amended by the Central Provinces Courts (Amendment) Act, 1935:-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A.-General</span></span><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_765\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/167753817/\">765.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">In these rules-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">\"Petition\" means a document written for the purpose of being presented to a criminal Court and includes a complaint and petition of appeal.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">\"To practise as a petition-writer\" means to write petitions as defined above for hire, and includes the writing of a single petition for hire.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">A petition-writer is said to practise in a Court when he writes petitions for the purpose of being presented to that Court.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_766\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/156804606/\">766.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No person shall practise as a petition-writer in the Criminal Courts of the province unless he has been duly licensed under these rules :</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Provided-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_766.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/33208049/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that any person licensed under any rule hitherto in force shall be deemed to have been licensed under these rules;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_766.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/7356082/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that a legal practitioner or his clerk shall not be considered to practise as a petition-writer, in respect of any petition written by the legal practitioner or by his clerk on his behalf, for presentation to a Court in which the legal practitioner is qualified to practise: provided that when the petition is written by a clerk it shall be signed by his employer.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_767\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/144130507/\">767.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No petition shall be rejected merely on the ground that it has been written by a person who is not a licensed petition-writer. Every petition shall show clearly the name and designation of the person by whom it has been scribed, and a Court may refuse to accept a petition not complying with this direction.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">B.-Licensing of Petition-Writers</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_768\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/191856214/\">768.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The number of licences granted under these rules shall be in accordance with the scale fixed for each district by the District Magistrate. The scale may be altered when necessary, but licences should not be granted indiscriminately without reference to the fixed scale.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_769\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/133784338/\">769.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any person above the age of 20 years may present a stamped application to the District Magistrate of the district in which he resides or desires to practise, to be licensed as a petition-writer.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_770\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/172092315/\">770.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_770.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/92527657/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The application shall be written by the applicant with his own hand and presented by him in person, and shall state-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_770.1.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/77072375/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the applicant's name, father's name, date of birth according to the English calendar, residence and present occupation (if any);</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_770.1.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/166836334/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the language or languages with which the applicant is acquainted;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_770.1.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/106945357/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the names of two respectable persons to whom reference may be made as to the applicant's character.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_770.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/49666626/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If the applicant has been convicted of a criminal offence or removed from Government service, this shall be stated in the application.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_770.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/142539980/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">If the applicant is in the service of Government or of a legal practitioner, his application shall state that he is prepared to resign such service on being licensed as a petitioner-writer. No person shall be licensed as a petition-writer whilst he is in the services of Government or of a legal practitioner.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_771\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/59768408/\">771.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">The District Magistrate to whom the application is made may, in his discretion, on being satisfied-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_771.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/95646638/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that the applicant is over 20 years of age,</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_771.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/82654497/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that he is of good character, and</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_771.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/85483968/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that he is otherwise eligible, grant the applicant a licence in Form A annexed to these rules.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_772\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/103994409/\">772.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every appointment shall be probationary in the first instance, and no probationer shall be confirmed until he satisfies the District Magistrate-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_772.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/161651732/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that he is able to draw up in a legible hand a clear and concise application, complaint or petition of appeal in the language of the Court in which he practises;</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_772.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/175146979/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">that he is acquainted with the provisions of the Penal Code, the Criminal Procedure Code, the Court-fees Act, the Stamp Act and the Limitation Act, so far as a knowledge of these Acts is necessary for the efficient performance of the duties of a petition-writer.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_773\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/23622118/\">773.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A register of licensed petition-writers in Form C annexed to these rules shall be maintained in the office of every District Magistrate. A page or pages of the register shall be set apart for each petition-writer.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">When a new register is opened, the superseded register shall be destroyed.</span><span class=\"akn-p\">C.-Conduct of Petition-Writers</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_774\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/29705098/\">774.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer shall maintain a register in Form B annexed to these rules and shall enter therein every petition written by him, and shall produce the register for the inspection of any judicial officer, when required to do so.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_775\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/69298396/\">775.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer shall, at his own expense, provide himself with an official seal of the following pattern :-</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Petitioner Writer</span><span class=\"akn-p\">Name.....................</span><span class=\"akn-p\">No.......................</span><span class=\"akn-p\">District.................</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_776\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/81375258/\">776.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer, in writing petitions, shall confine himself to expressing in plain and simple language such as the petitioner can understand and in a concise and proper form the statements and object of the petition, and shall not introduce any argument or quotation from a law report or other law book, or refer to any decision not brought to his notice by the petitioner.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_777\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/50567279/\">777.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer shall affix his seal (with his name and licence number filled in) on every petition written by him, and shall enter on such petition the number which it bears in his register and the fee which he has charged for writing it.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_778\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/59997945/\">778.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer shall re-write at his own cost any petition written by himself when required to do so by the order of a competent authority.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_779\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/82851223/\">779.</a> </h3>\n<section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_779.1\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/19745886/\">(1)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Subject to the provisions of Rule 782 every licensed petition-writer shall charge such fees only as may be prescribed by the District Magistrate. He shall note, in the petition as well as in the appropriate column of his register, the amount actually received by him.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_779.2\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/169388628/\">(2)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A licensed petition-writer shall not take payment for his services by an interest in the result of any litigation in connection with which he is employed and shall not fined, or contribute towards, the funds employed in carrying on any litigation in which he is not otherwise personally interested.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-subsection\" id=\"section_779.3\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/167911324/\">(3)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licensed petition-writer shall give to his employer a receipt for the amount received by him, specifying exactly what the money was received for, e.g., writing fees or costs and, if for costs, for what cost, e.g., complaint process-fees, etc. The details shall be set out separately either in the receipt itself or on a separate piece of paper attached to it.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_780\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/127395553/\">780.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">A licensed petition-writer shall not accept any mukhtyarnama, whether general or special for the conduct of any case in a Criminal Court other than a case in which he is himself a party.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_781\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/195881687/\">781.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Every licenced petition-writer-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_781.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/41444072/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">who resigns or is removed from his appointment, or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_781.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/42636180/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">who enters the service of Government or of an Indian State or of a legal practitioner, or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_781.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/173257748/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">who is suspended or dismissed under those rules, shall forthwith surrender his licence to the District Magistrate.</span></span></section><span class=\"akn-wrapUp\"><span class=\"akn-p\">D.-Procedure in dealing with Breaches of Rules</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_782\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/131643783/\">782.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any judicial officer who, upon the representation of any person employing a petition-writer, and after hearing such petition-writer (if he desires to be heard) finds that the fee charged for writing a petition presented in his Court was excessive may, by order in writing, reduce the fee to such sum as appears to be reasonable and proper, and may require the petition-writer to refund the amount received in excess of such sum. An order passed under this rule shall not be revised except by the officer who made it.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_783\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/109335590/\">783.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any judicial officer may order a licenced petition-writer to rewrite any petition written by him which contravenes Rule 776, or is illegible, obscure or prolix, or contains any irrelevant matter or misquotation, or is, from any other cause, in the opinion of such officer, informal or otherwise objectionable. An order passed under this rule shall not be revised except by the officer who made it.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_784\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/135431875/\">784.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any person who breaks Rule 766 shall be liable to a penalty not exceeding fifty rupees.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_785\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/46329470/\">785.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any licensed petition-writer, who breaks any of the Rules 774, 775, 777,779,780 and 781, shall be liable to a penalty not exceeding fifty rupees.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_786\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/29699637/\">786.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Breaches of rules specified in Rules 784 and 785 shall be cognizable by the District Magistrate. No penalty shall be inflicted in respect of such breaches unless the person charged has had an opportunity of defending himself.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_787\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/126608769/\">787.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any probationer who fails to satisfy the District Magistrate on the points mentioned in Rule 772, within one year from his being appointed a probationer is liable to be removed from his appointment by order of the District Magistrate.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_788\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/108309407/\">788.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Any licensed petition-writer who-</span></span><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.a\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/60475325/\">(a)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">habitually writes petitions contrary to Rule 776 or containing irrelevant matter or which are unnecessary or informal or otherwise objectionable; or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.b\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/3068334/\">(b)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">in the course of his business as a petition-writer uses disrespectful, insulting or abusive language; or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.c\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/78530198/\">(c)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">is found to be incapable of efficiently discharging the functions of a petition-writer; or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.d\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/58386839/\">(d)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">habitually remains absent during Court hours or is absent from his headquarters for a considerable period without sufficient cause; or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.e\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/144076800/\">(e)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">by reason of any fraudulent or improper conduct, is found to be unfit to practise as such; or</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-paragraph\" id=\"section_788.f\"><span class=\"akn-num\"><a href=\"/doc/90676205/\">(f)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">is convicted of a criminal offence;</span></span></section><span class=\"akn-wrapUp\"><span class=\"akn-p\">may be suspended or dismissed by order of the District Magistrate.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_789\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/196602575/\">789.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">No appeal shall lie from any order passed under any of the above rules.</span></span></section><section class=\"akn-section\" id=\"section_790\"><h3><a href=\"/doc/159088875/\">790.</a> </h3>\n<span class=\"akn-intro\"><span class=\"akn-p\">the High Court will exercise its general powers of superintendence and control with regard to orders passed under Rule 784, 785, 787 or 788 in the same manner as with regard to other administrative orders of the District Magistrate.</span><span href=\"/doc/7573431/\">(i)</a></span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Notification No. 9880-1115-28/60. - Notwithstanding any thing contained in the Rules and Orders (Civil) or Rules, and Orders (Criminal) or in any other previous orders the hours of work in every judicial office Civil of Criminal shall with immediate effect, and until further orders, be from 10-30 p.m. to 5 p.m. with a break of half an hour from 2 p.m. and 2-30 p.m. and a full holiday of second Saturday in a month.</span></span></section></section><section class=\"akn-section\"><h3>2. The High Court Notification No. 13356, dated the 13th December, 1962 is hereby superseded. [Published in M.P. Rajpatra Part I dated 8.1.1965 Page 85.]</h3>\n<section class=\"akn-paragraph\"><span class=\"akn-num\">(ii)</span><span class=\"akn-content\"><span class=\"akn-p\">Notification No. 143 dated the 5th January, 1966. - The High Court is pleased to extend, with the approval of the State Governor, Rules 415 to 421 of the Rules and Orders (Criminal) which are in force in the Mahakoshal Region of the State to the whole State. [Published in M.P. Rajpatra Part I, dated 17-6-1966 Page 1118.]</span></span></section></section></section></section></span></span>\n</div></span></span></div>\n\n\n\n\n\n</body></html>",
